| Goal | Tool |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
```

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

If MCP search returns no results:

# Kafka Consumer Group Rebalance Call Chain

## Your Task

Trace the Kafka consumer group rebalance protocol implementation across the Apache Kafka codebase. Find all Java source files in `apache/kafka` under `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/` that define or implement a class containing `Rebalance` in the class name. For each file, identify the class name and its role in the rebalance protocol (coordinator, assignor, callback handler).

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossrepo tracing domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kafka--0753c489, sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc, sg-evals/camel--1006f047.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/kafka--0753c489` (apache/kafka)
- `sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc` (apache/flink)
- `sg-evals/camel--1006f047` (apache/camel)

## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go"}
  ],
  "symbols": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "SymbolName"}
  ],
  "chain": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "FunctionName"}
  ],
  "text": "Narrative explanation of your findings, citing repos and file paths."
}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

## Evaluation

Your answer will be scored on:
- **File recall and precision**: Did you find all relevant files?

## Kafka Consumer Group Rebalance Protocol Implementation Analysis

I've traced the Kafka consumer group rebalance protocol implementation in the Apache Kafka codebase and identified **11 Java source files** under `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/` that define classes containing "Rebalance" in the class name.

### Files Found:

**Main Directory (5 files):**
1. **ConsumerRebalanceListenerInvoker.java** - Callback handler for invoking user-defined rebalance callbacks
2. **ConsumerRebalanceListenerMethodName.java** - Enum for rebalance listener method names
3. **StreamsRebalanceData.java** - Data container for Kafka Streams rebalance protocol
4. **StreamsRebalanceListener.java** - Interface for Streams task assignment callbacks
5. **StreamsRebalanceListenerInvoker.java** - Callback handler for Streams rebalance events

**Events Subdirectory (2 files):**
6. **ConsumerRebalanceListenerCallbackNeededEvent.java** - Event signaling callback is needed
7. **ConsumerRebalanceListenerCallbackCompletedEvent.java** - Event signaling callback completion

**Metrics Subdirectory (4 files):**
8. **RebalanceMetricsManager.java** - Abstract base for rebalance metrics
9. **ConsumerRebalanceMetricsManager.java** - Metrics coordinator for consumer rebalances
10. **ShareRebalanceMetricsManager.java** - Metrics coordinator for share group rebalances
11. **RebalanceCallbackMetricsManager.java** - Metrics for callback latency tracking

The complete analysis has been saved to `/workspace/answer.json` with detailed descriptions of each class's role in the rebalance protocol, organized by functional category (callback handlers, events, data/interfaces, and metrics).
